<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SIGNATURES</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pursuant to the requirements
of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, the registrant has duly caused this
report to be signed on its behalf by the undersigned hereunto duly authorized.</font></p>

<body lang="EN-US">

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit
99</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman"><img width="69" height="88" src="g43211mm01i001.jpg"></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 4.0in;text-indent:-4.0in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 4.0in;text-indent:-4.0in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">FOR
IMMEDIATE RELEASE</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 4.0in;text-indent:-4.0in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">TARGET CORPORATION ANNOUNCES</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">FOURTH QUARTER AND FISCAL 2009 EARNINGS</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">MINNEAPOLIS,
February&nbsp;23, 2010</font></b> -- Target Corporation (NYSE:TGT) today
reported net earnings of $936 million for the quarter ended January&nbsp;30,
2010, compared with $609 million in the quarter ended January&nbsp;31, 2009.
Earnings per share in the fourth quarter increased 53.3 percent to $1.24 from
81 cents in the same period a year ago. On a full year basis, earnings per
share were $3.30, a 15.2 percent increase from $2.86 in 2008. All earnings per
share figures refer to diluted earnings per share.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#147;We&#146;re very
pleased with our fourth quarter and full year 2009 financial performance, which
reflect substantial innovation and disciplined execution by teams across the
company,&#148; said Gregg Steinhafel, chairman, president, and chief executive
officer of Target Corporation. &#147;Fourth quarter retail segment performance was
well above our expectations due to stronger-than-expected holiday sales,
combined with well-controlled inventories and disciplined expense controls. In
2010, we expect our guest traffic trends and sales of discretionary categories
to benefit from broader implementation of our new merchandise initiatives as
well as a continued modest recovery in the economy, and believe Target will
continue to gain profitable market share.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Retail
Segment Results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Sales increased 3.7
percent in the fourth quarter to $19.7 billion in 2009 from $19.0 billion in
2008, due to the contribution from new stores and a 0.6 percent increase in
comparable-store sales. Retail segment earnings before interest expense and
income taxes (EBIT) were $1,560 million in the fourth quarter of 2009, an
increase of 24.7 percent from $1,251 million in 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Fourth quarter gross
margin rate increased 1.8 percentage points to 29.1 percent, driven by rate
improvement within categories slightly offset by the impact of faster sales
growth in non-discretionary, lower margin-rate categories. Category rate
favorability was driven in part by lower levels of clearance sales, which
declined more than 20 percent from the fourth quarter of 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Fourth quarter selling,
general and administrative (SG&amp;A) expenses increased 4.8 percent from
fourth quarter 2008, in line with expectations.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">For fiscal 2009, sales increased
0.9 percent to $63.4 billion from $62.9 billion in 2008, due to the
contribution from new stores, partially offset by a 2.5 percent decline in
comparable store sales. Full year retail segment EBIT increased 7.3 percent to
$4.4 billion in 2009 from $4.1 billion in 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Gross margin rate for
fiscal 2009 increased 0.7 percentage points to 30.5 percent, as rate
improvements within categories were partially offset by the impact of sales
mix. Fiscal 2009 selling, general and administrative (SG&amp;A) expense rate
was 20.5 percent, compared to 20.4 percent in 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">more --</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">TARGET
CORPORATION</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Page&nbsp;2</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Credit
Card Segment Results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Fourth quarter average
receivables decreased 10.2 percent to $8.1 billion in 2009 from $9.1 billion in
2008. Average receivables directly funded by Target declined 23.9 percent in
the fourth quarter to $2.7 billion from $3.6 billion in 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Fourth quarter bad debt
expense was $284 million in 2009, a 43.2 percent reduction from $500 million in
2008, when the company added significantly to its allowance for doubtful
accounts. Credit card segment profit for the quarter was $39 million, compared
with a loss of $135 million in fourth quarter 2008. Annualized segment pre-tax
return on invested capital was 5.7 percent in the fourth quarter 2009, compared
with negative 15.0 percent in 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Average receivables for
fiscal 2009 decreased 4.0 percent to $8.4 billion from $8.7 billion in 2008.
Average receivables directly funded by Target in 2009 declined 31.6 percent to
$2.9 billion from $4.2 billion in 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Full year 2009 segment
profit increased 29.4 percent to $201 million from $155 million in 2008. The
company added $6 million to the allowance for doubtful accounts in 2009. Full
year pre-tax return on the capital invested by Target in this segment was 7.0
percent in 2009, up from 3.7 percent in 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Interest
Expense and Taxes</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Net interest expense for
the quarter decreased $1 million from fourth quarter 2008, driven by lower
average debt balances offset by a higher average portfolio interest rate and a
$16 million charge related to the early retirement of debt.&#160; Full-year interest expense decreased $65
million from fiscal 2008, driven by a lower average portfolio interest rate
partially offset by a $16 million charge related to the early retirement of
debt.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">The company&#146;s effective
income tax rate for the fourth quarter was 33.5 percent in 2009. This rate is
approximately 3.5 to 4.0 percentage points less than the company&#146;s expected
annual long-term structural rate, due to a greater than normal portion of
earnings not subject to tax, and certain discrete state and federal
items.&nbsp; This lower provision for income taxes increased EPS by an amount
equal to approximately 7 cents per share in the quarter and for the year. For
the full year, the effective income tax rate was 35.7 percent, down from 37.4
percent in 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Share
Repurchase</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">In the fourth
quarter, under the share repurchase program originally announced in November&nbsp;2007
and resumed in January&nbsp;2010, the company repurchased approximately 8.3 million
shares of its common stock at an average price of $50.74, for a total
investment of $423 million.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Program-to-date
through the end of the fourth quarter, the company has acquired approximately
103.6 million shares of its common stock at an average price per share of
$51.36, reflecting a total investment of approximately $5.3 billion.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">--more --</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">TARGET
CORPORATION</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Page&nbsp;3</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Miscellaneous</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Target Corporation
will webcast its fourth quarter earnings conference call at 9:00am CST
today.&#160; Investors and the media are
invited to listen to the call through the company&#146;s website at
www.target.com/investors (click on &#147;events + presentations&#148; and then &#147;archives
+ webcasts&#148;). A telephone replay of the call will be available beginning at
approximately 11:30am CST today through the end of business on February&nbsp;25,
2010. The replay number is (800) 642-1687 (passcode: 49625661).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Statements in this
release regarding expected traffic, sales and market share gains are
forward-looking statements within the meaning of the Private Securities
Litigation Reform Act of 1995.&nbsp; Such statements speak only as of the date
they are made and are subject to risks and uncertainties&nbsp;which could
cause&nbsp;the company&#146;s&nbsp;actual results&nbsp;to differ materially.&nbsp;
The most important risks and uncertainties are described in&nbsp;Item
1A&nbsp;of the company&#146;s&nbsp;Form&nbsp;10-K for the fiscal year ended January&nbsp;31,
2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Target Corporation&#146;s
retail segment includes large general merchandise and food discount stores and
Target.com, a fully integrated on-line business. In addition, the company
operates a credit card segment that offers branded proprietary and Visa credit
card products. The company currently operates 1,740 Target stores in 49 states.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Target Corporation
news releases are available at www.target.com.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">###</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.0pt;font-style:italic;">EBITDA is earnings before interest
expense, income taxes, depreciation and amortization.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.0pt;font-style:italic;">EBIT is earnings before interest
expense and income taxes.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:6.5pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">(a)</font></i><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font></i><i><font size="1" style="font-size:9.0pt;font-style:italic;">New account and loyalty
rewards redeemed by our guests reduce reported sales. Our Retail Segment
charges the cost of these discounts to our Credit Card Segment, and the reimbursements
of $29 million and $89 million for the three and twelve months ended January&nbsp;30,
2010, respectively, and $41 million and $117 million for the three and twelve
months ended January&nbsp;31, 2009, respectively, are recorded as a reduction
to SG&amp;A expenses within the Retail Segment.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:2.0pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:-2.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:4.5pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:-2.0pt;">(a)</font></i><i><font size="1" style="font-size:4.5pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:-2.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></i><i><font size="1" style="font-size:7.0pt;font-style:italic;">New account and loyalty
rewards redeemed by our guests reduce reported sales. Our Retail Segment
charges the cost of these discounts to our Credit Card Segment, and the
reimbursements of $29 million and $89 million for the three and twelve months
ended January&nbsp;30, 2010, respectively, and $41 million and $117 million for
the three and twelve months ended January&nbsp;31, 2009, respectively, are
recorded as an increase to operations and marketing expenses within the Credit
Card Segment.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:4.5pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:-2.0pt;">(b)</font></i><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font></i><i><font size="1" style="font-size:7.0pt;font-style:italic;">Amounts represent the
portion of average gross credit card receivables funded by Target. These
amounts exclude $5,412 million and $5,484 million for the three and twelve
months ended January&nbsp;30, 2010, respectively, and $5,484 million and $4,503
million for the three and twelve months ended January&nbsp;31, 2009,
respectively, of receivables funded by nonrecourse debt collateralized by
credit card receivables.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:-2.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:4.5pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:-2.0pt;">(c)</font></i><i><font size="1" style="font-size:7.0pt;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;ROIC is return on invested
capital, and this rate equals our segment profit divided by average gross
credit card receivables funded by Target, expressed as an annualized rate.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:4.5pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:-2.0pt;">(d)</font></i><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font></i><i><font size="1" style="font-size:7.0pt;font-style:italic;">As an annualized
percentage of average gross credit card receivables.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:4.5pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:-2.0pt;">(a)</font></i><i><font size="1" style="font-size:7.0pt;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;Balance-weighted
one-month LIBOR</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:4.5pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:-2.0pt;">(b)</font></i><i><font size="1" style="font-size:7.0pt;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;As a percentage of
average gross credit card receivables.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:4.5pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:-2.0pt;">(c)</font></i><i><font size="1" style="font-size:7.0pt;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;Spread to LIBOR is a metric
used to analyze the performance of our total credit card portfolio because the
vast majority of our portfolio earned finance charge revenue at rates tied to
the Prime Rate, and the interest rate on all nonrecourse debt securitized by
credit card receivables is tied to LIBOR.</font></i></p>
